***трясти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a> (3564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tręstì</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trjastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тряхнуть.html>тряхну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to jolt, to shake (of a vehicle, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be shaking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясёт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>trjasjót</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is shaking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shake out
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вытрясти.html>вы́трясти</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výtrjasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>тря<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сти́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>Трясти́</a> кого-то (что-то) <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> кем-то (чем-то).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-тряс-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***трястись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a> (3169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trjastísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trjastísʹ</b> ot sméxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tremble, to shiver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясётся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vesʹ <b>trjasjótsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is trembling allover</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лода</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trjastísʹ</b> ot xóloda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shiver with cold</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trjastísʹ</b> ot stráxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to quake with fear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадка.html>лихора́дке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trjastísʹ</b> v lixorádke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shiver with fever</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be jolted, to ride something jolty</li>
<li>to tremble <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трястись.html>трясти́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:копейка.html>копе́йкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trjastísʹ</b> nad káždoj kopéjkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to watch every penny</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туалет.html>туале́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tualét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tualétnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toilet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tualétnaja</b> bumága</i> ― <span class="e-translation">toilet paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tualétnaja</b> vodá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">toilet water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мыло.html>мы́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tualétnoje</b> mýlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scented soap <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for washing face and hands</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>toilet</b> soap</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:столик.html>сто́лик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tualétnyj</b> stólik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dressing table <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туалет.html>туале́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tualét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тугой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тугой.html>туго́й</a> (5457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тугъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tugŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tǫgъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hard, strong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tengʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тугой.html>туго́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tugój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ту́же</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tight, taut <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">under high tension</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тугой.html>туго́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tugój</b> na úxo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hard of hearing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тугой.html>туго́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***тулуп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>тулу́п</a> (9489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from Turkic or some other Altaic language. The exact origin and its jaunt, per Vasmer, is hard to ascertain given that the borrowing is found in other Slavic languages such as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ту́луб</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túlub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>ту́луп</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túlup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. A more distant cognate is <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">tulum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>тулу́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tulúp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>тулу́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>тулу́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тулуп.html>тулу́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sheepskin coat, overcoat, tulup (Russian-style long warm sheepskin/hareskin coat with a collar)</li></ol>

***туман.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a> (1442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested since the 17th century.
Borrowed from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source. Ultimately, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Turkic language">Proto-Turkic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="trk-pro">*dum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬛𐬎𐬥𐬨𐬀𐬥</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dunman</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fog, mist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬛𐬎𐬎𐬄𐬥𐬨𐬀𐬥</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duuąnman</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">duman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">тұман</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tuman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">томан</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">دود</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dūd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">دودمان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dūdmān</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke, soot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tumán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fog
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́не</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ kak v <b>tumáne</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>to be in a fog</i> (state of mind)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ну</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">napustítʹ <b>tumánu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to equivocate<i>; </i>to beat around the bush</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***туманный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:туманный.html>тума́нный</a> (5266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tumán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туманный.html>тума́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tumánnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тума́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тума́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fog</li>
<li>foggy, misty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obscure, nebulous, vague, unclear</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мана.html>ма́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>тума́ннее, тума́нней.</i>

***тумба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a> (12018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tumbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grave, coffin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tumba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">túmba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мбы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cupboard, cabinet, pedestal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кухонный.html>ку́хонная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kúxonnaja <b>túmba</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">base unit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>túmba</b> písʹmennovo stol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">desk cupboard</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">прикроватная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prikrovatnaja <b>túmba</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">bedside table</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>advertising pillar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stone <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to bind horses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fat/rotund person, tub</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумбочка.html>ту́мбочка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">túmbočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумбочка.html>ту́мбочки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумбочка.html>ту́мбочки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумбочка.html>ту́мбочек</a></b>)

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тумба.html>ту́мба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túmba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (low) cabinet</li>

***тунеядец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дец</a> (17613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound formed from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">тоуне</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tune</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> 'given freely; for no purpose' (also found in the adverb <a href = vnd.unilang:втуне.html>втуне</a>), and *ядец, 'eater' (related to <a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еда</a> 'food').
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tunejádec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дцев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тунея́дка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>idler, parasite, freeloader
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1860</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoyevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Dostoyevsky">Fyodor Dostoyevsky</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/An_Honest_Thief" class="extiw" title="w:An Honest Thief">An Honest Thief</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пьянчужка.html>пьянчу́жка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a>, потаску́н, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тунеядец.html>тунея́дец</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прежде.html>пре́жде</a> где́-то, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уж.html>уж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выключить.html>вы́ключили</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pʹjančúžka takój, potaskún, <b>tunejádec</b> služíl préžde gdé-to, da jevó za pʹjánuju žiznʹ už davnó iz slúžby výključili.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A drunk and a rake, the <b>idler</b> had served somewhere in the past but had been expelled from service long ago for his drunken lifestyle.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:туника.html>туни́ка</a> (28685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tunica</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>тупик</a> (5166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупой.html>тупо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tupój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>ту́пик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">túpik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>ту́пика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>ту́пики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупик.html>ту́пиков</a></b>)
